                                    <p>Verse SS.6.1.26 and 27 are not in sequence and mixed up with
                                        each other. Folio no 353r has a few words in the margin
                                        below which I couldn’t find where to add them.</p>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Madhududan Rimal"> 6.41 from NAK 5-333: the ending of
                                    the chapter is: uttaratantre śoṣacikitsā aṣṭatriṃsattamaḥ
                                    kāyacikitsāyāṃ tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ || So it looks like it is being
                                    called chapter 38, not 41. </note>

                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">
                                    <list>
                                        <item>1) I have doubt about the chapter number as the
                                            colophon of the manuscript mentions:
                                            "uttaratantre'ṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyāṃ
                                            yonivyāpaccikitsā trayoviṅśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ||"
                                            As I have understood it, the above heading is given to
                                            the subject of this mail . I have also marked the same
                                            in the transcription file. Please comment.</item>
                                        <item>2) The folios which I have transcribed i.e 480r:3,
                                            480v, 481r, 481v are not paginated.</item>
                                        <item>3) Missing verses: 6.38.2, 3, 4, 5ab, 5cd, 5, 6, 7,
                                            6.38.30ab, 32cd, 32ef Probably, 6.38.4.1 is left out to
                                            mark in the vulgate copy, like other verses 6.38.3.1,
                                            6.38.2 etc. which are in manuscript. I am not sure about
                                            this observation. In vulgate, verse number 6.38.8.1 is
                                            shown as missing but in manuscript I could not find
                                            different text relating to that for addition. (Here,
                                            also I may be wrong.)</item>
                                        <item>4) Additions: 6.38.3.1, 3.2, 4.1, 5.1, 6.1, 7.1</item>
                                        <item>5) SS. 6.38.8cd, 17 cd , 23cd, 26cd, 27cd - the second
                                            half has different text.</item>
                                        <item>6) SS.6.38.28 ab - the first half has different
                                            text.</item>
                                    </list>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Vandana Lele"> This adhyaya is numbered 47 in the
                                    vulgate and 44.9 in NAK 5-333 <list>
                                        <item>1) Missing verses: 6.47.2, 6.47.4cd, 6.47.11, 12,

                                        <item>3) Special Notes: <list>
                                                <item>i) The text of 6.47.4a and 4b added by me is
                                                  intermingled with 6.47.4cd which is shown missing
                                                  by me.</item>
                                                <item>ii) 6.47.20cd - the second half verse has
                                                  different text.</item>
                                                <item> iii) 6.47.38 - the first half verse has
                                                  different text. </item>
                                                <item>iv) 6.47.43cd and 44ab - the text is
                                                  intermingled i.e. 43.cd has only a word whereas
                                                  44ab has rest of the text.</item>
                                                <item>v) The Letter-numerals given on the folios are
                                                  not noted by me in the transcription. </item>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.1"><pb n="3434V"/>
                        <lb n="3"/>athāto raktapittapratiṣedham vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>





                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.3x">vyāyāmabhārādhyayana<lb n="4"/>vyavo yātapasevanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇoṣṇakṣāralavaṇair amlaiḥ kaṭvabhir eva ca <cb/> ||</l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.4x">abhīkṣṇaṃ sevato tyuṣṇo rasaḥ pittam pradūṣayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittam vidagdhaṃ svaguṇair vvidahatyāśu śoṇitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.5">tataḥ <lb n="5"/>pravattate raktam ūrdddhañ cādho dvidhāpi
                        vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         āmāsayād vrajed ūrdhvam a<cb/>dhaḥ pakvāsayād rahet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6ab">vidagdhayoś cāpy ubhayor dvidhābhāgam pravarttena |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7ab">ūrdhvan sādhyamadhoyāpyamasādhyaṃ yuga<lb n="6"
                        />padgataṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.6cd">yakṛn plīhāsyām ichanti kecid raktagatiṃ janāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.7cd">sadanaṃ śītakāmitvaṃ kaṇṭhadhūmāyanaṃ vamiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.8">lohagandhiś ca niśvāso bhavaty asmin bhaviṣyati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vāhyāsṛglakṣaṇais tasya sa<pb n="3424R"/>
                        <lb n="1"/>khyā doṣocchritair vviduḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.9">daurvvalyaṃśvāsakāsajvaravamathumadā pāṇḍutādāhamūrcchā
                        bhukte cānne vidāhas tv adhṛtir api sadā
                        hṛdyatulyā<unclear>va</unclear>pīḍā|
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇā kaṇṭhasya bhedaḥ śirasi ca pa<lb n="2"/>vanaṃ pūtiniṣṭhīvanañ ca
                        <caesura/>
                         dveṣo bakte vipāko viratir api bhavad ra<cb/>ktapittopasargāt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.10">mānsaprakṣālanābhaṃ kvathitam api yakṛtkarddamāmbhonibham
                        vā medaḥ pūyāsthikalpaṃ <lb n="3"/>yakṛd iva yadi vā pakvajambūphalābhaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yat kṛṣṇaṃ yac ca nīlabhṛśama<cb/>tikuṇapaṃ yatra coktā vikārās tad varjyaṃ
                        raktapittaṃ surapatidhanuṣā yac ca tulyam vibhāti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.11">nodṛktam ādau<lb n="4"/>saṃgrhyāṃ valinobhiṣajā sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛt pāṇḍugrahaṇīroga plīhagu<cb/>lmajvarāvahaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.12">adhaḥ pravṛttam vamanair ūrddhagan tu virecanaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jayed anyatarañ <unclear>cā</unclear>pi kṣīṇasya śamanai<lb n="5"/>r asṛk
                        ||</l>





                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.15">drākṣākāśmaryamadhuka sitāyetam virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yaṣṭhī<cb/>madhukasiddhañ ca sakṣaudram vamanaṃ hitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.16">payāṃsi śītāni rasāś ca jāṅgalāḥ satīnamūdgāyavaśā<pb
                            n="6"/>liṣaṣṭikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvanti śailūsuniṣaṇṇayūthikāṃs tathātimuktāṃṅkurasinduvārajāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.17">śākaṃ hitan sarppiṣisaṃskṛtaṃ sadā pathyāñ ca
                        dhātrīphaladāḍimānvitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāś ca pārāvatahaṃ<pb n="3425V"/>
                        <lb n="1"/>sakurmmajajāḥ peyās tathā cāpi ghṛtāntarā hitāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.18">sāntānikāś cotpalapūrvvakeṣu ghṛteṣu siddhāḥ payasaḥ sitā
                            <unclear>.</unclear>ḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         himāpradehāmadhurāgaṇāś ca ghṛtāni pathyāni ca raktapitte ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.19"><lb n="2"/>madhūkasaubhāñjanakodirajaiḥ priyaṅgukānāṃ
                        kusumaiś ca cūrṇṇitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣag vidadhyāc caturaḥ samākṣikāṃ hitāya lehānasṛjaḥ praśāntaye ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.20">lihyāc ca dugdhadrumajān na vā<lb n="3"/>
                        <unclear>.</unclear>rān madhudvitīyāṃ sitakarṇṇikasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyāñ ca kharjjūraphalaṃ samā<cb/>kṣikaṃ phalāni cānyānyapitaṅguṇānyathā
                        ||</l>

                    <l n="SS.6.45.21ab">raktātisārābhihitānyogān atrāpi yojayet |</l>

                         peved akṣasamaṅ kalkaṃ madhukasyaivameva vā |</l>

                        <caesura/>
                         pathyā caivāvapīḍeṣu<lb n="2"/> grāṇataḥ pramṛte 'sṛji ||

                        <caesura/>
                         yakṛd vā bhakṣayed ājā māṃsaṃ pittasamāyutaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.45.29">palāśavṛntasvarase vipakvaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         sarppiḥ pi<lb n="3"/>vet kṣaudrayutaṃ hitāśī ||
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.48.1"> athātastṛṣṇāpratiṣedhamadhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyā<cb/>maḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.36">ayaś cūrṇāsyatrai<g ref="#new-gap-filler"/><pb n="469v"/>
                        levā vi <unclear reason="faded">dhi</unclear>nāyojayīt ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakāṃsanīlaṃ tailaṃ ca nasyaṃ syāt suranādike || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.37"> indraluptavidhiś cāpi vidheyo romavājiṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         dantājānāṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ vidhānaṃ mukharogike <lb n="2"/>|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.38"> raktajānāṃ pratīkāraṃ <unclear>ku</unclear>ryāt
                        kuṣṭhacikitsitat |
                        <caesura/>
                         surasādiś ca <cb/>sarvvaṣu sarvvathaivopayojayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.54.39"> pravyaktatikatakaṭukaṃ bhojanañ ca hitaṃ sada |
                        <caesura/>
                        <unclear>ku</unclear> latharasasaṃyuktaṃ<gap extent="1" unit="char"/>
                        kṣārapānañ ca pūjitam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.1"> athāto viśūcikāpratiṣedham vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.3"> ajīrṇṇam āmaṃ viṣṭabdham vi<pb n="473r(98r)"/><lb n="1"
                        />dagdhaṃ ca yad īritaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśūcyalasakau tasmād bhavec cāpi viḍambikā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.4"> sūcībhir iva gātrāṇi tudan santiṣṭhate 'nilaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasyām ajīrṇṇāt sā vaidyair vvisūcīti nirucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.5"> na tāṃ parimitāhārā <lb n="2"/>labhante viditāgamāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūḍhās tām ajitātmāno labhante <add place="top margin">śana<metamark
                                function="line-number-from-top">2</metamark></add>lolupāḥ <cb/>|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.6"> mūrcchātisārau vamathuḥ pipāsā
                        śūlabhramodveṣṭanajṛmbhadāhāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaivarṇṇyakampau hṛdaye rujaś ca bhavanti tasyāṃ <lb n="3"/>śirasaś ca
                        bhedaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.7"> kukṣir ānahyate 'tyarthaṃ tāmyate parikūjati |
                        <caesura/>
                        <cb/>niruddho mārutaś caiva<metamark function="yati">,</metamark> kukṣāv
                        upari dhāvati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.8"> vātavarcco nirodhaś ca<metamark function="yati"
                            >,</metamark> kukṣau yasya bhṛśam bhavet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasyālasaka<lb n="4"/>m ācaṣṭe<metamark function="yati">,</metamark>
                        tṛṣṇodgārau ca yasya tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.9"> duṣṭañ ca bhuktaṅ kaphamārutābhyāṃ<g
                            ref="#newa-gap-filler"/>
                        <cb/>pravarttate norddhvam adhaś ca yasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         viḍambikān tasya suduścikitsyām ācakṣate śāstravidaḥ purāṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.56.10"> yatrastha<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><lb n="5"/>m āmaṃ hi
                        rujārttam eva deśaṃ viśeṣeṇa vikārajātaiḥ |

                         yathā yo brūyāt pattrasā iti || <lb n="5"/>vādī tac ca prati pratipādyāt tū

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.29"> pra<cb/>karaṇān tū pūrvvyād abhihitaṃ vidhānam ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā <subst><del>śakti</del>
                            <add place="bottom-margin">sakthi<metamark
                                    function="line-number-from-below"
                        >2</metamark></add></subst>marmmāṇy ekādaśa prakaraṇāt tū pūrvvyā<gap
                            reason="blank" extent="3" unit="char"/>ni || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.30"> evaṃ <lb n="6"/>vakṣyatīty anāgatāpekṣaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ślokasthāne brūyāc cikitsyeṣu vakṣyāmīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.31"> ity uktam atikrāntāpekṣaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā cikitsiteṣu brūyāc chlokasthāne yad abhihitam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.32"> ubhayantattū<pb n="413v"/><lb n="1"/>nidarśanaṃ saṃśayaḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā lahṛdayaghātaḥ prāṇaharaḥ pāṇipādacchedanam aprāṇaharaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.33"> tatrātimayo 'pavarṇṇanaṃ vyākhyānaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatheha pañcaviṅśakaḥ <gap reason="blank" extent="3" unit="char"/>
                        vyākhyāyate | tathā nānyeṣv āyurvve<lb n="2"/>datantreṣu sutādim
                        pratyārabdhaś cintā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.34"> anyaśāstrāsāmānyā <cb/>svajñā <gap reason="blank"
                            extent="2" unit="char"/>ṣu tantreṣu saṃjñā yā svasaṃjñā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yatheha śāstre mithunam iti | madhusarppiṣo grahaṇaṃ trivṛtam i<lb n="3"
                        />ti | sarppistailavasā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.35"> lokaprathitam udāharaṇaṃ nirvvacanaṃ |
                        yatho<cb/>ṣṇabhayāc chām antūsarati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.36">dṛṣṭāntavyaktir nnirvvacanaṃ | yathā agnir vvāyusahi<gap
                            reason="blank" extent="12" unit="char"/><lb n="4"/><gap reason="blank"
                            extent="3" unit="char"/>phaduṣṇo vraṇo bhivṛddhiṃ gacchatīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.37"> idam eveti niyo<g ref="#newa-gap-filler"/><cb/>gaḥ |
                        yathā pathyam eva bhoktavyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.39"> idam evedañ ceti vikalpaḥ | yathā māṃsavargge
                            eṇahariṇalāva<lb n="5"/>tittirāḥ pradhānā īti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.38"> saṃkṣepa vacanaṃ ca samuccayaḥ | <gap reason="blank"
                            extent="several" unit="char"/></l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.6.65.40"> tad iṣṭaṃ buddhigamyan tad ūhyaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         ya<gap reason="blank" extent="5" unit="char"/><lb n="6"/><gap

                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcānyena anne bhakṣyam aviruddhad yena sādharmmyāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvvidhas tv āharaḥ | praviralaḥ prāyeṇa dvividha eva ca | āto
                            dvitvaprasiddha<gap extent="4" unit="char"/> | </l>
